   sukhābhāvo nānabhivyaktirasti, ubhayasya nityatvāt/	suKa aBAvaH na anaBivyakti rasti, uBayasya nitya tvAt/

   nāsti, kāraṇasya nityatvāt, tathā saṃsārasthasyāpīti|	nAsti, kAraNasya nitya tvAt, taTA saMsAra sTasya api iti|

   gṛhyeteti//	gRhyeta iti//

   etaccāyuktam, śarīrādaya upabhogārthāste bhogapratibandhaṃ kariṣyantītya	etat ca ayuktam, SarIra AdayaH upaBoga arTAH te Boga pratibanDam karizyanti iti a
   nupapannam |	nupapannam |

   NyS_1,1.36: sādhyasādharmyāt taddharmabhāvī dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇam //	NyH _1,1.36: sADya sADarmyAt tad Darma BAvI dRzwAntaH udAharaNam //
   sādhyena sādharmyaṃ samānadharmatā|	sADyena sADarmyam samAna Darma tA|
   sādhyasādharmyātkāraṇāttaddharmabhāvī dṛṣṭānta iti|	sADya sADarmyAt kAraNAt tad Darma BAvI dRzwAntaH iti|
   tasya dharmastaddharmaḥ|	tasya DarmaH tad DarmaH|

   tasya dharmastaddharmaḥ|	tasya DarmaH tad DarmaH|
   taddharmasya bhāvastaddharmabhāvaḥ|	tad Darmasya BAvaH tad Darma BAvaH|
   sa yasmin dṛṣṭānte vartate sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ taddharmabhāvī|	sa yasmin dRzwAnte vartate sa dRzwAntaH tad Darma BAvI|
   yasmin dṛṣṭānte sādhyasādharmyādutpattidharmakatvāt sādhyasya dharmo	yasmin dRzwAnte sADya sADarmyAt utpatti Darmaka tvAt sADyasya DarmaH 
   'nityatvaṃ bhavati sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ|	anitya tvam Bavati sa dRzwAntaH|
   sādhyasādharmyādutpattidharmakatvāttaddharmabhāvī bhavati, sa	sADya sADarmyAt utpatti Darmaka tvAt tad Darma BAvI Bavati, sa
   codādaharaṇamiṣyate|	ca udAda haraNam izyate|

   tatra yudatpadyate tadutpattidharmakam|	tatra yudat padyate tad utpatti Darmakam|
   tacca bhūtvā na bhavati, ātmānaṃ jahāti nirudhyata ityanityam|	tat ca BUtvA na Bavati, AtmAnam jahAti niruDyate iti anityam |

   upalabhyate|	upalaByate|

   NyS_1,2.13: sambhavato 'rthasyātisāmānyayogād asambhūtārthakalpanā	NyH _1,2.13: samBavataH arTasya ati sAmAnya yogAt asamBUta arTa kalpanA

   NyS_4,2.34: smṛtisaṃkalpavacca svapnaviṣayābhimānaḥ //	NyH _4,2.34: smRti saMkalpavat ca svapna vizaya aBimAnaH //

   svapnānto jāgaritāntena|	svapna antaH jAgarita antena|

   saṃkṣepeṇoktaṃ tadvistareṇa vibhajate, tāḥ khalvimā jātayaḥ sthāpanāhetau	saMkzepeNa uktam tad vistareNa viBajate, tAH Kalu imAH jAtayaH sTApana ahetO
   prayukte caturviṃśatiḥ pratiṣedhahetavaḥ |	prayukte caturviMSatiH pratizeDa hetavaH |
   NyS_5,1.1:	NyH _5,1.1:
   sādharmyavaidharmyotkarṣāpakarṣavarṇyāvarṇyavikalpasādhyaprāptyaprāptiprasaṅgapratidṛṣṭāntānutpattisaṃśayaprakāraṇāhetvarthāpattyaviśeṣopapattyupalabdhyanupalabdhinityānityakāryasamāḥ	sADarmya vEDarmya utkarza apakarza varNyAvarNya vikalpa sADya prApti aprApti prasaFga pratidRzwAnta anutpatti saMSaya prakAraNA hetu arTApatti avi
   sādharmyeṇa pratyavasthān aviśiṣyamāṇaṃ syāpanāhetutaḥ sādharmyasamaḥ,	sADarmyeNa pratyavasTAn aviSizyamANam syApanAhetutaH sADarmya samaH,
   viśeṣaṃ tatra tatrodāhariṣyāmyaḥ, evaṃ vaidharmyasamaprabhṛtayopi	viSezam tatra tatra udAharizyAmi aH, evam vEDarmya sama praBRtayA upi
   nirvaktavyāḥ // 1 //	nirvaktavyAH // 1 //

   NyS_5,1.2: sādharmyavaidharmyābhyāmupasaṃhāre taddharmaviparyayopapatteḥ	NyH _5,1.2: sADarmya vEDarmyAByAm upasaMhAre tad Darma viparyaya upapatteH
   sādharmyavaidharmyasamau //	sADarmya vEDarmya samO //
   sādharmyeṇopasaṃkāre sādhyadharmviparyayopapatteḥ sādharmyeṇaiva	sADarmyeNa upasaMkAre sADya Darmviparyaya upapatteH sADarmyeNa eva
   pratyavasthānam aviśiṣyamāṇaṃ sthāpanāhetutaḥ sādharmyasamaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ,	pratyavasTAnam aviSizyamANam sTApanA hetutaH sADarmya samaH pratizeDaH,
   nidarśanam   'kriyāvānātmā   dravyasya kriyaḥhetuguṇayogāt. dravyaṃ loṣṭaḥ	nidarSanam  akriyAvAn AtmA  dravyasya kriyaH hetu guNa yoga at. dravyam lozwaH
   kriyāhetuguṇayukta kriyāvān tathā cātmā tasamāt kriyāvān' iti,	kriyA hetu guNa yukta kriyAvAn taTA ca AtmA tasamAt kriyAvAn a iti,
   evamupasaṃhṛte paraḥ sādharmyeṇaiva pratyavatiṣṭhate   'niṣkriya ātmā  	evam upasaMhRte paraH sADarmyeNa eva pratyavatizWate   anizkriyaH AtmA  
   vibhuno dravyasya niṣkriyatvāt. vibhu cākāśaṃ niṣkriyaṃ ca tathā cātmā	viBunaH dravyasya nizkriya tvAt. viBu ca AkASam nizkriyam ca taTA ca AtmA
   tasmāt niṣkriyaḥ' iti, na cāsti viśeṣahetuḥ   kriyāvatsādharmyāt kriyāvatā	tasmAt nizkriyaH a iti, na ca asti viSeza hetuH  kriyAvat sADarmyAt kriyAvatA
   bhavitavyaṃ na purakriyasādharmyād niṣkriyeṇeti, viśeṣahetvabhāvān	Bavitavyam na pura kriya sADarmyAt nizkriyeNa iti, viSeza hetu aBAvAn
   sādharmyasamāḥ pratiṣedho bhavati|	sADarmya samAH pratizeDaH Bavati|
   atha vaidharmyasamaḥ   'kriyāhetuguṇayukto loṣṭaḥ paricchinno dṛṣṭo na	aTa vEDarmya samaH  akriyA hetu guNa yuktaH lozwaH paricCinnaH dRzwaH na
   tathātmā tasmānna loṣṭavat kriyāvān' iti. na nāsti viśeṣahetuḥ  	taTA AtmA tasmAt na lozwa vat kriyAvAn a iti. na na asti viSeza hetuH  
   kriyāvatsādharmyāt kriyāvatā bhavitavyaṃ na punaḥ	kriyAvat sADarmyAt kriyAvatA Bavitavyam na punar 
   kriyāvadvaidharmyādkiyeṇeti. viśeṣahetvabhāvād vaidharmyasamaḥ|	kriyAvat vEDarmyAt kiyeNa iti. viSeza hetu aBAvAt vEDarmya samaH|
   vaidharmyeṇa copasaṃhāre   'niṣkriya ātmā   vibhutvāt. kriyāvad	vEDarmyeNa ca upasaMhAre  anizkriyaH AtmA  viBu tvAt. kriyAvat 
   dravyamavibhu dṛṣṭaṃ yathā loṣṭaḥ na ca tathātmā tasmād niṣkriyaḥ' iti,	dravyam aviBu dRzwam yaTA lozwaH na ca taTA AtmA tasmAt nizkriyaH a iti,
   vaidharmyeṇa pratyavasthānam   'niṣkriyaṃ dravyamākāśaṃ	vEDarmyeNa pratyavasTAnam   anizkriyam dravyam AkASam
   kriyāhetuguṇarahitaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ na tathātmā tasmānna niṣkriyaḥ' iti. ni cāsti	kriyA hetu guNa rahitam dRzwam na taTA AtmA tasmAt na nizkriyaH a iti. ni ca asti
   viśeṣahetuḥ   kriyāvadvaidharmyād niṣkriyeṇa bhavitavyaṃ na	viSeza hetuH  kriyAvat vEDarmyAt nizkriyeNa Bavitavyam na
   punarakriyavaidharmyāt kriyāvateti. viśeṣahetvabhāvād vaidharmyasamaḥ|	punar akriya vEDarmyAt kriyAvatA iti. viSeza hetu aBAvAt vEDarmya samaH|
   atha ( punaḥ ) sādharmyasamaḥ   'kriyāvān loṣṭaḥ kriyāhetuguṇayukto dṛṣṭaḥ	aTa ( punar ) sADarmya samaH  akriyAvAn lozwaH kriyA hetu guNa yuktaH dRzwaH
   tathā cātmā tasmātpava kriyāvān' iti. na cāsti viśeṣahetuḥ  	taTA ca AtmA tasmAt pava kriyAvAn a iti. na ca asti viSeza hetuH  
   kriyāvadvaidharmyād niṣkriyo na punaḥ kriyāvatsādharmyāt kriyāvāniti.	kriyAvat vEDarmyAt nizkriyaH na punar kriyAvat sADarmyAt kriyAvAniti.
   viśeṣahetvabhāvāt sādharmyasamaḥ // 2 //	viSeza hetu aBAvAt sADarmya samaH // 2 //

   NyS_5,1.3: gotvādgosiddhivattatsiddhiḥ //	NyH _5,1.3: go tvAt go sidDi vat tad sidDiH //
   sādharmyamātreṇa vaidharmyamātreṇa ca sādhyasādhane pratijñāyamāne	sADarmya mAtreNa vEDarmya mAtreNa ca sADya sADane pratijQAyamAne
   syādavyavasthā sā tu dharmaviśeṣe nopapadyate, gosādharmyād	syAt avyavasTA sA tu Darma viSeze na upapadyate, go sADarmyAt 
   gotvājjātiviśeṣād gauḥ sidhyati na tu sāsnādisaṃbandhāt. aśvādivaidharmyād	go tvAt jAti viSezAt gOH siDyati na tu sAsnAdi saMbanDAt. aSva Adi vEDarmyAt 
   gotvādeva gauḥ sidhyati na guṇādibhedāt, taccaitat	go tvAt eva gOH siDyati na guNa Adi BedAt, tat ca etat 
   kṛtavyākhyānamavayavaprakaraṇe, pramāṇānāmabhisaṃbandhāccaikārthakāritvaṃ	kRta vyAKyAnam avayava prakaraNe, pramANAnAm aBisaMbanDAt ca eka arTa kAri tvam
   samānaṃ vākye iti, hetvābhāsāśrayā khalv iyam avyavastheti // 3 //	samAnam vAkye iti, hetvABAsa ASrayA Kalu iyam avyavasTA iti // 3 //

   NyS_5,1.4: sādhyadṛṣṭāntayordharmavikalpādubhayasādhyatvācca	NyH _5,1.4: sADya dRzwAntayoH Darma vikalpAt uBaya sADya tvAt ca
   utkarṣāpakarṣavarṇyāvarṇyavikalpasādhyasamāḥ //	utkarza apakarza varNyAvarNya vikalpa sADya samAH //
   dṛṣṭāntadharma sādhye samāsajata utkarṣasamaḥ   yadi	dRzwAnta Darma sADye samAsajataH utkarza samaH  yadi
   kriyāhetuguṇayogalloṣṭavat kriyāvānātmā ( tadā ) loṣṭavadeva sparśavānapi	kriyA hetu guNa yogat lozwa vat kriyAvAn AtmA ( tadA ) lozwa vat eva sparSavAn api
   prāpnoti. atha na sparśavān loṣṭavat kriyāvānapi na prāpnoti, viparyaye vā	prApnoti. aTa na sparSavAn lozwa vat kriyAvAn api na prApnoti, viparyaye vA
   viśeṣo vaktavya iti|	viSezaH vaktavyaH iti|
   sādhye dharmābhāvaṃ dṛṣṭāntāt prasajato 'pakarṣasamaḥ   loṣṭaḥ khalu	sADye Darma aBAvam dRzwAntAt prasajataH apakarza samaH  lozwaH Kalu
   kriyāvān avibhurdṛṣṭaḥ kāmamātmāpi kriyāvānavibhurastu. viparyaye vā	kriyAvAn aviBuH dRzwaH kAmam AtmA api kriyA vAn aviBuH astu. viparyaye vA
   viśeṣo vaktavya iti|	viSezaH vaktavyaH iti|
   khyāpanīyo varṇyo viparyayādavarṇyaḥ tāvetau sādhyadṛṣṭāntadharmauṃ	KyApanIyaH varNyaH viparyayAt avarNyaH tO= etO sADya dRzwAnta Darma om
   viparyasyato varṇyāvarṇyasamau bhavataḥ|	viparyasyataH varNyAvarNya samO BavataH|
   sādhanadharmayukte dṛṣṭānte dharmāntaravikalpāt sādhyadharmavikalpaṃ	sADana Darma yukte dRzwAnte Darma antara vikalpAt sADya Darma vikalpam
   prasajato vikalpasamaḥ   kriyāguṇahetuyuktaṃ kiñcid guru yathā loṣṭaḥ	prasajataH vikalpa samaH  kriyA guNa hetu yuktam kiQcid guru yaTA lozwaH
   kiñcicca laghu yathā vāyurevaṃ kriyāhetuguṇayuktaṃ kiñcat kriyāvat syād	kiQcid ca laGu yaTA vAyuH evam kriyA hetu guNa yuktam kiQcat kriyAvat syAt 
   yathā loṣṭaḥ kiñcidakriyaṃ yathātmā. viśeṣo vā vācya iti|	yaTA lozwaH kiQcid akriyam yaTA AtmA. viSezaH vA vAcyaH iti|
   hetvādyivayavasāmarthyayogī dharmaḥ sādhyastaṃ dṛṣṭānte prasajataḥ	hetu Adi iva yava sAmarTya yogI DarmaH sADyaH tam dRzwAnte prasajataH
   sādhyasamaḥ   yadi 'yathā loṣṭastathātmā ?' prāptastarhi 'yathātmā tathā	sADya samaH  yadi ayaTA lozwaH taTA AtmA ?a prAptaH tarhi ayaTA AtmA taTA
   loṣṭaḥ' iti. sādhyaścāyamātmā kriyāvāniti kāmaṃ loṣṭopi sādhyaḥ, atha	lozwaH a iti. sADyaH ca ayam AtmA kriyAvAn iti kAmam lozwopi sADyaH, aTa
   naivam ? na tarhi 'yathā loṣṭastathātmā' (iti ) // 4 //	na evam ? na tarhi ayaTA lozwaH taTA AtmAa (iti ) // 4 //

   idaṃ tāvadayaṃ pṛṣṭo vaktumarhati   atha ke pradīpamupādadate kimarthaṃ	idam tAvat ayam pRzwaH vaktum arhati  aTa ke pradIpam upAdadate kim arTam

   NyS_5,1.12: prāgutpatteḥ kāraṇābhāvādanutpattisamaḥ //	NyH _5,1.12: prAk utpatteH kAraNa aBAvAt anutpatti samaH //
   anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatnānantarīyakatvād ghaṭavadityukte apara āha  	anityaH SabdaH prayatna anantarIyaka tvAt Gawa vat iti ukte aparaH Aha  
   prāgutpatteranutpanne śabde prayatnānantarīyakatvamanityatvakāraṇaṃ nāsti	prAk utpatteH anutpanne Sabde prayatna AnantarIyaka tvam anitya tva kAraNam na asti
   tadabhāvād nityatvaṃ prāptaṃ nityasya cotpattirnāsti|	tad aBAvAt nitya tvam prAptam nityasya ca utpattiH na Asti|
   anutpattyā pratyavasthānam anutpattisamaḥ // 12 //	anutpattyA pratyavasTAnam anutpatti samaH // 12 //

   NyS_5,1.13: tathābhāvādutpannasya kāraṇopapatterna kāraṇapratiṣedhaḥ //	NyH _5,1.13: taTA aBAvAt utpannasya kAraNa upapatteH na kAraNa pratizeDaH //
   tathābhāvādutpannasyeti   utpannaḥ khalvayaṃ śabda iti bhavati.	taTA aBAvAt utpannasya iti  utpannaH Kalu ayam SabdaH iti Bavati.
   prāgutpatteḥ śabda eva nāsti   utpannasya śabdabhāvāt. śabdasya sataḥ	prAk utpatteH SabdaH eva nAsti  utpannasya Sabda BAvAt. Sabdasya sataH
   prayatnānantarīyakatvam anityatvakāraṇamupapadyate.	prayatna AnantarIyaka tvam anitya tva kAraNam upapadyate.
   kāraṇopapatterayuktoyaṃ doṣaḥ  	kAraNa upapatteH ayuj toyam dozaH  
   "prāgutpatteḥ kāraṇābhāvāt"iti // 13 //	"prAk utpatteH kAraNa aBAva at"iti // 13 //

   NyS_5,1.14: sāmānyadṛṣṭāntayoraindriyakatve samāne nityānityasādharmyāt	NyH _5,1.14: sAmAnya dRzwAntayoH Endriyaka tve samAne nitya anitya sADarmyAt

   pratyavatiṣṭhate   sati prayatnānāntarīyakatve astyevāsya nityena	pratyavatizWate  sati prayatnAnAntarIyaka tve asti eva asya nityena
   sāmānyena sādharmyam  aindriyakatvam. asti ca ghaṭenānityena. ato	sAmAnyena sADarmyam Endriyaka tvam. asti ca Gawena anityena. atas

   NyS_5,1.15: sādharmyātsaṃśaye na saṃśayo vaidharmyād ubhayathā vā saṃśaye	NyH _5,1.15: sADarmyAt saMSaye na saMSayaH vEDarmyAt uBayaTA vA saMSaye
   'tyantasaṃśayaprasaṅgo nityatvānabhyupagamācca sāmānyasyāpratiṣedhaḥ //	atyanta saMSaya prasaFgaH nitya tva anaByupagamAt ca sAmAnyasya apratizeDaH //
   viśeṣād vaidharmyādavadhāryamāṇe 'rthe 'puruṣaḥ' iti na	viSezAt vEDarmyAt avaDAryamANe arTe apuruzaH a iti na

   NyS_5,1.16: ubhayasādharmyāt prakriyāsiddheḥ prakaraṇasamaḥ //	NyH _5,1.16: uBaya sADarmyAt prakriyA sidDeH prakaraNa samaH //
   ubhayenaunityena cānityena sādharmyāt pakṣapratipakṣayoḥ pravṛttiḥ	uBayena Onityena ca anityena sADarmyAt pakza pratipakzayoH pravRttiH
   prakriyā, 'anityaḥ śabdaḥ prayatnānantarīyakatvād ghaṭavat' ityekaḥ pakṣaṃ	prakriyA, aanityaH SabdaH prayatna anantarIyaka tvAt Gawavat a iti ekaH pakzam
   pravartayati. dvitīyaśca nityasādharmyāt. evaṃ ca sati	pravartayati. dvitIyaH ca nitya sADarmya at. evam ca sati
   'prayatnānantarīyakatvāt' itiheturanityasādharmyeṇocyamāno na	aprayatna anantarIyaka tvAt a iti hetuH anitya sADarmyeNa ucyamAnaH na
   prakaraṇamativartate. prakaraṇānativṛtternirṇayānanivartanam, samānaṃ	prakaraNam ativartate. prakaraNa anati vRtteH nirNayAna nivartanam, samAnam
   caitannityasādharmyeṇocyamāne hetau, tadidaṃ prakaraṇānativṛttyā	ca etat nitya sADarmyeNa ucyamAne hetO, tat idam prakaraNa anativRttyA
   pratyavasthānaṃ prakaraṇasamaḥ|	pratyavasTAnam prakaraNa samaH|
   samānaṃ caitadvaidharmye 'pi = ubhayavaidharmyāt prakriyāsiddheḥ	samAnam ca etat vEDarmye api  uBaya vEDarmyAt prakriyA sidDeH
   prakaraṇasama iti // 16 //	prakaraNa samaH iti // 16 //

   bhavati, yadyubhyasādharmyaṃ tatraikataraḥ pratipakṣa ityevaṃ	Bavati, yadi uBya sADarmyam tatra ekataraH pratipakzaH iti evam
   satyupapannaḥ pratipakṣo bhavati. pratipakṣopapatteranupapannaḥ	sati upapannaH pratipakzaH Bavati. pratipakza upapatteH anupapannaH
   pratiṣedhaḥ   yataḥ pratipakṣopapattiḥ pratiṣedhopapattiśceti	pratizeDaH  yatas pratipakza upapattiH pratizeDa upapattiH ca iti
   vipratiṣiddhamiti|	vipratizidDam iti|

   tattvāvadhāraṇe hyavasitaṃ prakaraṇaṃ bhavatīti // 17 //	tattva avaDAraNe hi avasitam prakaraNam Bavati iti // 17 //

   hetuḥusādhanaṃ tat sādhyāt pūrvaṃ paścāt saha vā bhavet. yadi pūrvaṃ	hetuHusADanam tat sADyAt pUrvam paScAt saha vA Bavet. yadi pUrvam
   sādhanam ? asati sādhye kasya sādhanam, atha paścāt ? asati sādhane	sADanam ? asati sADye kasya sADanam, aTa paScAt ? asati sADane
   kasyedaṃ sādhyam, atha yugapat sādhyasādhate ? dvayorvidyamānayoḥ kiṃ	kasya idam sADyam, aTa yugapad sADya sADate ? dvayoH vidyamAnayoH kim
   kasya sādhanaṃ kiṃ kasya sādhyam. iti heturahetunā na viśiṣyate|	kasya sADanam kim kasya sADyam. iti hetuH ahetunA na viSizyate|

   nityapakṣasya hāniriti|	nitya pakzasya hAniH iti|
   anekāntikatvāccārthāpatteḥ = ubhayapakṣasamā ceyamarthāpattiḥ   yadi	aneka antika tvAt ca arTApatteH  uBaya pakza samA ca iyam arTApattiH  yadi
   nityasādharmyādasparśatvādākāśavacca nityaḥ śabdaḥ ? ( tadā )	nitya sADarmyAt asparSa tvAt AkASa vat ca nityaH SabdaH ? ( tadA )

   ceyaṃ viparyayamātrādekāntenārthāpattiḥ. na khalu vai dhanasya grāvṇaḥ	ca iyam viparyaya mAtrAt ekAntena arTApattiH. na Kalu vE Danasya grAvNaH

   NyS_5,1.23: ekadharmopapatteraviśeṣe sarvāviśeṣaprasaṅgāt sadbhāvopapatter	NyH _5,1.23: eka Darma upapatteH aviSeze sarva aviSeza prasaFgAt sadBAva upapatteH 
   aviśeṣasamaḥ //	aviSeza samaH //
   eko dharmaḥ prayatnānantarīyakatvaṃ śabdaghaṭayorupapadyate ityaviśeṣe	ekaH DarmaH prayatna AnantarIyaka tvam Sabda GawayoH upapadyate iti aviSeze

   katham ? sadbhāvopapatteḥ = eko dharmaḥ sadbhāvaḥ sarvasyopapadyate|	kaTam ? sadBAva upapatteH  ekaH DarmaH sadBAvaH sarvasya upapadyate|

   NyS_5,1.24: kvaciddharmānupapatteḥ kvaciccopapatteḥ pratiṣedhābhāvaḥ //	NyH _5,1.24: kvacid Darma anupapatteH kvacid ca upapatteH pratizeDa aBAvaH //
   yathā sādhyadṛṣṭāntayorekadharmasya	yaTA sADya dRzwAntayoH eka Darmasya
   prayatnānantarīyakatvasyopapatteranityatvaṃ dharmāntaram aviśeṣo naivaṃ	prayatna anantarIyaka tvasya upapatteH anitya tvam Darma antaram aviSezaH na evam

   atha matam   anityatvameva dharmāntaraṃ sadbhāvopapattinimittaṃ bhāvānāṃ	aTa matam  anitya tvam eva Darma antaram sadBAva upapatti nimittam BAvAnAm
   sarvatra syāditi ?, evaṃ khalu vai kalpyamāne   'anityāḥ sarve bhāvāḥ	sarvatra syAt iti ?, evam Kalu vE kalpyamAne  aanityAH sarve BAvAH
   sadbhāvopapatteḥ' itipakṣaḥ prāpnoti, tatra	sadBAva upapatteH a iti pakzaH prApnoti, tatra
   pratijñārthavyatiriktamanyadudāharaṇaṃ nāsti. anudāharaṇaśca heturnāstīti,	pratijQA arTa vyatiriktam anyat udAharaNam nAsti. anudAharaNaH ca hetuH na asti iti,
   pratijñaikadeśasya codāharaṇatvamanupapannam   na hi sādhyamudāharaṇaṃ	pratijQa eka deSasya ca udAharaNa tvam anupapannam  na hi sADyam udAharaNam
   bhavati, sataśca nityānityabhāvādanityatvānupapattistasmāt	Bavati, sataH ca nitya anityaBAvAt anitya tva anupapattiH tasmAt 
   'sadbhāvopapatteḥ sarvāviśeṣaprasaṅgaḥ' iti nirabhidheyametadvākyamiti|	asadBAva upapatteH sarva aviSeza prasaFgaHa iti niraBiDA iyam etat vAkyam iti|
   'sarvabhāvānāṃ sadbhāvopapatteranityatvam' iti bruvatānujñātaṃ	asarva BAvAnAm sadBAva upapatteH anitya tvam a iti bruvata anujQAtam
   śabdasyānityatvaṃ tatrānupapannaḥ pratiṣedha iti // 24 //	Sabdasya anitya tvam tatra anupapannaH pratizeDaH iti // 24 //

   NyS_5,1.26: upapattikāraṇābhyanujñānādapratiṣedhaḥ //	NyH _5,1.26: upapatti kAraNa aByanujQAnAt apratizeDaH //
   "ubhayakāraṇopapatteḥ"itibruvatā nānityatvakāraṇopapatteranityatvaṃ	"uBaya kAraNa upapatteH"itibruva tA na anitya tva kAraNa upapatteH anitya tvam
   pratiṣidhyate, yadi pratiṣidhyate ? nobhayakāraṇopapattiḥ syāt|	pratiziDyate, yadi pratiziDyate ? na uBaya kAraNa upapattiH syAt |

   ? spapakṣaparapakṣayoḥ samāno vyāghātaḥ sa ca naikatarasya sādhaka iti //	? spapakza para pakzayoH samAnaH vyAGAtaH sa ca na ekatarasya sADakaH iti //
